  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_8e62f65f-f1e0-48eb-830b-35ad50fe2dfd'
      });
    }

  <span id="freeText6226621841926074993" style="display:none"><i>“When Day and Night combine and fight against one Enemy,<br />then Dark and Light shall meet mid-strike and set the Captives free.”</i><br /><br />In the wake of loss and devastation, Alex must cast aside her grief to seek aid from those who banished the Meyarins long ago. But the proud Tia Aurans care little for the woes of mortals and demand that Alex—and her friends—undergo the Gates of Testing to prove their world is worth saving.<br /><br />With an ancient prophecy looming, Alex must confront the secrets of her past if she is to survive long enough to see the future. For if she returns to Medora without the Tia Aurans by her side, all hope will be lost.<br /><br />In this explosive conclusion to <i>The Medoran Chronicles</i>, the fate of Medora hangs in the balance as Alex readies herself to face Aven one final time.<br /><br />Who will survive, and who will fall?<br /><br /><i>“If, however, darkness wins, there is no strategy<br />to keep from all that will be lost, and so will always be.”</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12327947120471757514"><b>I'M DONE.</b><br/><br/>It's all over, and my heart is breaking.<br/><br/>I don't know what comes next in my life, now?<br/><br/>I mean, other than, like, <i>a billion re-reads.</i><br/><br/>***<br/><br/>To be honest, I'm not sure I'm going to write a review for this one.<br/><br/><b>I don't know if I can.</b><br/><br/>I went into this knowing nothing but the same cliffhanger we all got with <i>Graevale</i>, and I want that experience to be the same for everyone else who reads this book.<br/><br/>I think if you've come this far, you've earned it.<br/><br/>So I'm not going to say anything about the plot. Or th</span>
  <span id="freeText12327947120471757514" style="display:none"><b>I'M DONE.</b><br /><br />It's all over, and my heart is breaking.<br /><br />I don't know what comes next in my life, now?<br /><br />I mean, other than, like, <i>a billion re-reads.</i><br /><br />***<br /><br />To be honest, I'm not sure I'm going to write a review for this one.<br /><br /><b>I don't know if I can.</b><br /><br />I went into this knowing nothing but the same cliffhanger we all got with <i>Graevale</i>, and I want that experience to be the same for everyone else who reads this book.<br /><br />I think if you've come this far, you've earned it.<br /><br />So I'm not going to say anything about the plot. Or the characters. Or the moments I loved or loathed.<br /><br />I <b>will</b> say that I loved this book.<br /><br />I <b>will</b> say it was just as emotional as I expected it to be.<br /><br />There were highs; there were lows.<br /><br />I had to pause often because things were getting so intense.<br /><br />This is a worthy conclusion to an absolutely incredible story, and it has firmly taken up residence in my heart. The world of Medora is so rich and thriving with colour and magic and so many incredible characters that I'm certain we'll have the chance to return there one day.<br /><br />For now, though, I'm sad to say goodbye, but I'm so grateful for this book, and how everything played out. It felt ... right.<br /><br />And I have so much love for these characters that even though I don't want to leave them, I think they have earned their rest.<br /><br />***<br /><br />Review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23569787.Akarnae__The_Medoran_Chronicles___1_" title="Akarnae (The Medoran Chronicles, #1) by Lynette Noni" rel="nofollow noopener">Akarnae</a> (4★s) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1631335573" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a><br />Review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26077971.Raelia__The_Medoran_Chronicles___2_" title="Raelia (The Medoran Chronicles, #2) by Lynette Noni" rel="nofollow noopener">Raelia</a> (5★s) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1841687518" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a><br />Review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29570559.Draekora__The_Medoran_Chronicles___3_" title="Draekora (The Medoran Chronicles, #3) by Lynette Noni" rel="nofollow noopener">Draekora</a> (5★s) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1841687530" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a><br />Review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35439559.Graevale__The_Medoran_Chronicles___4_" title="Graevale (The Medoran Chronicles, #4) by Lynette Noni" rel="nofollow noopener">Graevale</a> (5★s) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2031039032" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a><br />Review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/38459424.We_Three_Heroes__The_Medoran_Chronicles___4_5_" title="We Three Heroes (The Medoran Chronicles, #4.5) by Lynette Noni" rel="nofollow noopener">We Three Heroes</a> (4★s) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2502505830" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13271000203383144963">I am a mess of emotions and I don't think I'll be able to get my thoughts and feelings across in a coherent review so bullet points for the win.<br/><br/>• Straight up this book made me cry not once, not twice, but three times!!! I have stressed previously how rare this is for me. I did the maths. Around 2% of the books I read make me cry, and <b>two</b> books from that series are a part of that 2%. And again, <b>three times!!</b> <br/>• Not only did this book made me cry, I was even laughing while crying at one point. Like</span>
  <span id="freeText13271000203383144963" style="display:none">I am a mess of emotions and I don't think I'll be able to get my thoughts and feelings across in a coherent review so bullet points for the win.<br /><br />• Straight up this book made me cry not once, not twice, but three times!!! I have stressed previously how rare this is for me. I did the maths. Around 2% of the books I read make me cry, and <b>two</b> books from that series are a part of that 2%. And again, <b>three times!!</b> <br />• Not only did this book made me cry, I was even laughing while crying at one point. Like, how?!?<br />• Pretty much this book made me an emotional mess and I had <b>ALL THE FEELS. <u>ALL OF THEM.</u></b><br />• As always, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/9857504.Lynette_Noni" title="Lynette Noni" rel="nofollow noopener">Lynette Noni</a> managed to write incredibly beautiful and vivid worlds that will forever stick in my brain and make me jealous that I can't actually visit them. <br />• This book was a bit predictable at times but it also managed to wallop me over the head as well so...<br />• Kaidan. I fucking love the dude, and he's the epitome of respectful, loveable, strong, mature, kind-hearted, amazing, I could go on love interest, but he's a little too perfect. I don't think I spotted a single flaw in him in this book. <br />• Dragons!! Well, Draekons, but semantics. Dragons!!<br />• <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[That reunion with Xira was exactly what I wanted and I didn't even realise it. Ugh *Italian chef kiss* perfection. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />• Alex. I love her to bits, but she can be a bit dumb at times. I'm trying to put it down to the fact that she had the literal weight of a world hanging on her shoulders, so you could say her mind was a bit preoccupied, but still. Think woman, think!<br />• <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I would have loved it if Bear &amp; Declan were confirmed to be together in this book, but at the same time I definitely think their relationship will be a slow burn one and will need more time than this book allowed to develop. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />• Read the acknowledgements at the end and thank me later because:<br />• <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b>THERE WILL BE MORE BOOKS ABOUT MEDORA!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!</b> Thank fucking god. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />• Did... Did <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/9857504.Lynette_Noni" title="Lynette Noni" rel="nofollow noopener">Lynette Noni</a> just hint that she'd be releasing <b>three</b> books this year? Omg, pls pls pls. I need. <br /><br />And with that I wrap up my most amazing, highly professional review that eloquently, and <s>actually does</s> succinctly convey my thoughts about this book. I fucking love it. <br /><br /><br /><br /><u>
  <b>14th January 2019</b>
</u><br />I have been following the author on Facebook for ages now, and only just realised this has been pushed back until February 18th. <div id="review_2720031772" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2720031772" />
    <a title="Ryan Buckby" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32429909-ryan-buckby"><img alt="Ryan Buckby" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528436487p2/32429909.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2720031772?book_show_action=true">Mar 03, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ryan Buckby" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ryan Buckby" href="/user/show/32429909-ryan-buckby">Ryan Buckby</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2720031772" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11308807205924028034"><b> First read: March 3rd 2019 </b><br/><b> Re-read: March 11th 2020 </b><br/><br/><b>Don’t fear the shadows. Make the shadows fear you. </b><br/><br/><br/>What a way to end this fantastic that i have come to love and enjoy over the last three and half years, thank you Lynette for writing this amazing series. <br/><br/><br/><b> Plot: </b> This book picks up after the events from the pervious book and Alex is now making her way to Tia Auras to try get the people to come join her fight against Aven and hopefully end up winning this war. I have really enjoyed reading th</span>
  <span id="freeText11308807205924028034" style="display:none"><b> First read: March 3rd 2019 </b><br /><b> Re-read: March 11th 2020 </b><br /><br /><b>Don’t fear the shadows. Make the shadows fear you. </b><br /><br /><br />What a way to end this fantastic that i have come to love and enjoy over the last three and half years, thank you Lynette for writing this amazing series. <br /><br /><br /><b> Plot: </b> This book picks up after the events from the pervious book and Alex is now making her way to Tia Auras to try get the people to come join her fight against Aven and hopefully end up winning this war. I have really enjoyed reading this story and watching it grow from where we first met Alex and how much of a long this story has matured and gone. <br /><br />Most of this book is spent in Tia Auras where Alex and her friends must compete in 6 different task that will test them and finally get help from the civilisation living there. A lot of these challenges test Alex with not only herself but also her friends, i did love how everything was brought into the open and everyone started to learn the truth with how things became so bad. <br /><br />Alex for the all of this book is trying to fight between doing what is right and what is wrong but also is trying to fight her emotions after the traumatic fight that took place in the pervious book that resulted in the deaths of some pretty important characters. I think the biggest death that Alex struggled with the most with was Nyix because of how much of a close bond they had with each other and for me it was the hardest death apart from Bear's dad that left me crying. <br /><br /><br />I love Alex and how big her friends mean to her and friendship plays such a big role in this story and all the friendships are so well written that it makes me want to be apart of that friendship group. Alex relies on her friends as her friends rely on her for all different sort of things which i found to be so heart warming. <br /><br /><br /><b> may the light be your guide. </b> <br /><br /><br /><b> Characters: </b><br /><br /><b> Alex Jennings: </b> Alex has matured so much since the first book and she has kept her composure so well even when things are revealed with everyone which makes her such a strong female lead. She fights with so much in this book because she literally has the world at her shoulders with trying to literally save every single life from Aven but she is managing to keep her sh*t together real well and more than i would ever be able to. <br /><br />Alex and Kaiden also have a very flirty relationship in this book and more than any of the others and i'm glad that Alex finally let her guard down with him and finally let him in more. These two have been back and fourth ever since he was introduced in book three and i'm glad that they are finally together. <br /><br /><br />Alex made one of the biggest and ballsy moves i thought that she made in the entire series and that was to trap Aven in a painting rather than kill him. I feel like this was the most mature and adult thing i could have ever imagined for any YA character so i give props to Lynette for writing this for Alex to do. <br /><br /><br /><b> Jordan Sparker: </b> Along with the other main group of characters i think Jordan has been through nearly everything imaginable and probably more. Jordan is still trying to come down from being claimed by Aven which to me is still really sitting heavy on his mind and rightly so. <br /><br /><br />Jordan doesn't get anytime to relax however because he is thrown with Alex into the Tia Auran's world where he is also put to the test with the task they have been set. I think about time it was time for Jordan to finally learn the truth with how Alex claimed him and set him free but he also doesn't take this well which is a normal reaction but he soon sees sense and apologises to Alex and i think as i said before these characters have all matured so much since the first book its great to see them making adult decisions. <br /><br /><br />After Jordan finds out his father was never claimed by Aven i think he does the mature thing and decides to stay away from his mother after all the horrible things they did to him as he was growing up, However i would like to see a reunion between him and his mother so i could find out how his mum felt about what they did to him. <br /><br /><br /><b> Bear Ronnigan: </b> Bear is one of my favourite characters in this entire series and i was with him when his father was killed and i was equally upset that it happened. I think Bear does a lot holding back in this one due to him still trying to process the death of his dad but i still find it so brave of him for coming to help Alex in her quest. <br /><br /><br />Bear gets help from all of his friends in different ways which i found so good because each friend was bringing help in their own different ways. I do however found that Declan and Bear had a little something going on but i'm not sure if i'm reading into that a little to much it was just an observation that i had i could be really wrong though. <br /><br /><br />It was good to see how Bear dealt with his dads passing in We three heroes and i was glad his family supported him with going to help Alex and i really just love the whole Ronnigan family. <br /><br /><br /><b> Delucia Cavelle aka D.C: </b> D.C along with Bear is one of my favourite characters of this series and it's good to see a royal princess turn out to be this badass fighter who is capable of not just sitting from the sidelines and actually getting into the fighting to save her kingdom. I love the change D.C has had from the first book where she is reserved and very nasty towards everyone to see her in this final book where she has a friendship with Alex, Bear, Kaiden and Declan and a relationship with Jordan its a very big change. <br /><br />As i said in my Graevale review the change D.C has shown with showing us her stand off persona to becoming this warrior type princess who's ready to fight aven and his army and do the dirty work where most princess would be just sitting back waiting for the war to be over not D.C she's the total opposite which is why i like her. <br /><br />Jordan and D.C are just one of the best pairings i've had the chance to read and of course at first i didn't think it would work as i said in my Graevale review but during the course of this book i've come to see how they really do care for each other and are ready to fight for each other its just amazing how powerful Lynettes story telling is. <br /><br /><br /><b> Kaiden James: </b> I really enjoyed the fact that Kaiden was introduced as not the main characters love interest straight way because it would have ruined this characters image for me. I'm glad we slowly get to know Kaiden from when he's introduced right up until this last book where he really proves himself a lot. <br /><br /><br />Kaiden has proven himself time and time again all throughout this series with how much of a capable fighter he is. At first i wasn't on board with Alex and Kaiden but as i read the other books these two just work really well together and even though there very different to each other they just fit. <br /><br /><br />During Vardaesia i think Kaiden really helps keep Alex grounded and helps her during the tough decisions she has to make but doesn't outrightly push her in one direction he just simply guides her and brings her back if she thinks she can't do anything which i really loved. <br /><br /><br /><b> Declan Stirling: </b> Declan is the best friend of Kaiden and these two are joined at the hip while at Akarnae so it's only natural that he would accompany Kaiden and help Alex during her test that she has to do. Declan is one of those friends who is always willing to help people and knows just the right thing to say in any different situation which i found a great thing to have. <br /><br /><br />Declan really helps bear in this book a lot as Declan has dealt with the deaths with most of his family so i think these two really hit if off straight away. I do have a little feeling that these two might have been a thing that wasn't outwardly said but implied but i could be really wrong. <br /><br /><br /><br /><b> Aven Dalmarta: </b> Aven is one of those characters that i love to hate for various reasons and especially when Alex goes back in time and he really got me liking him in book three where Alex accidentally does something that puts Aven on this past to kill humans. <br /><br /><br />Aven is such a cunning character though because he can get you to like him straight away but as soon as you peal away those layers that this character has you start to see what a complete psycho he really his but he also does it in a charming way. I'm glad that Aven didn't get the huge death that most books like this have but i think he should defiantly suffer in that painting after everything he had done. <br /><br /><b>Is, was, and forever will be, Alex mused. And I thought the Library couldn’t get any more mysterious </b> <br /><br /><br />This book had so much death as in a war you'd expect but it still pulled at my heart strings and made me cry in so many different parts of this book and Lynettes writing for this series has been exceptional. <br /><br />The scene with Alex and Nyix was one of my most favourite in this book because Nyix just knows the right things to say to Alex to get her to keep fighting when she wants to give up, it was a truly beautiful final scene these two got to share. <br /><br /><br />Well that comes to an end on Alex's story and i'm sad but incredibly happy with how things were wrapped up i could have not asked for a better ending to this part of the story. I almost threw my book to learn that Lynette will be writing in this world again so the story will continue very soon and i will welcome this world back into my life when this does happen. <br /><br /><br />But for now i will say goodbye to Alex, Jordan, Bear, D.C, Kaiden, Declan and the rest of the characters from the Medoran Chronicles who i've come to love over the last three and half years. This isn' the end and i'm happy it's not.<br /><br /><b>To those who dare hope for a brighter future. Let your light shine. </b><br /><br />and remember <br /><br /><b>
  <i> Embrace The Wonder </i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="11308807205924028034" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13196671959640373546">This book really broke me. And everytime I reread it, it breaks me a little bit more. And I reread it A LOT.<br/><br/>I can't believe this series is over. I love this series so, so much and I thank Lynette Noni for writing it.   <span id="freeText13196671959640373546" style="display:none">This book really broke me. And everytime I reread it, it breaks me a little bit more. And I reread it A LOT.<br /><br />I can't believe this series is over. I love this series so, so much and I thank Lynette Noni for writing it. So much love. <br /><br />Firstly, this book was the perfect ending to the series. Page turning and funny, with the cutest romance, this book was amazing. And the plot twists and reveals, just wow. I just have to say, Kaiden and Alex are one of my ultimate favourite ships because god, those two are everything. They're so freaking perfect. And don't even get me started on Bear and Declan from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/38459424.We_Three_Heroes__The_Medoran_Chronicles___4_5_" title="We Three Heroes (The Medoran Chronicles, #4.5) by Lynette Noni" rel="nofollow noopener">We Three Heroes</a>. Those two better have a spin off storyline, I swear to god....<br /><br />The characters were done as perfectly as always, with amazing personalities and some real tough moments for the gang. The writing was thrilling as always, and my only wish is to have gotten more of the combat boys. I truly loved them. Lynette Noni managed to capture my heart with this series, and for that I will always thank her. <br /><br />I loved this series and this book so much. I cried a HEAP <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ God I loved the combat boys. I intend to reread it several times and cry, laugh and scream (from happiness and fear) some more. (And I have definitely done that). <br /><br />Do yourself a favour and read this series.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2365313683?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mary-ellen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mary-ellen" href="/user/show/8288505-mary-ellen">Mary-ellen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2365313683" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2540805212583500773">Having read the first four books in rapid succession (and with little sleep) about a year ago, I couldn’t wait to get my hands on the final book in The Medoran Chronicles, Vardaesia, and I’m glad to say it did not disappoint.<br/><br/>The first half of this book has Alex and Kaiden travelling to Tia Auras to enlist their help in the upcoming showdown with Aven. Alex and her friends are put through a series of tests to prove themselves, and while there Alex learns some new things about the ancient prophecy</span>
  <span id="freeText2540805212583500773" style="display:none">Having read the first four books in rapid succession (and with little sleep) about a year ago, I couldn’t wait to get my hands on the final book in The Medoran Chronicles, Vardaesia, and I’m glad to say it did not disappoint.<br /><br />The first half of this book has Alex and Kaiden travelling to Tia Auras to enlist their help in the upcoming showdown with Aven. Alex and her friends are put through a series of tests to prove themselves, and while there Alex learns some new things about the ancient prophecy. They return to Medora to discover that Aven has not been idle in their absence. His evil escalates, leading to the ultimate violent showdown between Alex and Aven. <br /><br />Vardaesia is full of action, revelations, reunions and romantic developments. But best of all it has a killer ending. There are some surprises along the way, and I loved how Lynette Noni wrapped this story up. While I’m sad that this series has come to an end, Noni has signalled her plans to revisit Medora in the future, so I’ll look forward to that. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2540805212583500773" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

The Medoran Chronicles has been an Australian institution for the last four years and five books and a novella series later, it's finally come to an end. From Akarnae to Vardaesia, to the heights of the Draekorans above the City of Meya, Lynette Noni has captivated and delighted readers with her unlikely group of heroes and enchantingly atmospheric world of Medora, it's been a privilege. </span>

<div id="review_2818272992" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2818272992" />
    <a title="Wayne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32087829-wayne"><img alt="Wayne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1458869186p2/32087829.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2818272992?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wayne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wayne" href="/user/show/32087829-wayne">Wayne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2818272992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer95285013869270143">All the stars I can give it<br/><br/>This series has been amazing and it's a bit sad that it's over really.<br/><br/>I remember starting it and thinking that it was just a standard YA read with standard YA tropes but it just hooked me.<br/><br/>The world building Is a massive part of that. Just phenomenal. So many different worlds, so many of the same worlds but different. Just amazing writing that transports you there.<br/><br/>The characters though are the true stars here. Alex Is such a great leader and I love how she's not perfect</span>
  <span id="freeText95285013869270143" style="display:none">All the stars I can give it<br /><br />This series has been amazing and it's a bit sad that it's over really.<br /><br />I remember starting it and thinking that it was just a standard YA read with standard YA tropes but it just hooked me.<br /><br />The world building Is a massive part of that. Just phenomenal. So many different worlds, so many of the same worlds but different. Just amazing writing that transports you there.<br /><br />The characters though are the true stars here. Alex Is such a great leader and I love how she's not perfect. She's always in it up to her neck but her fighting spirit and never say die attitude is inspirational. I also love the friendships and how that bond is stressed as such an important thing. Bear, Jordan, Kaiden, and also Avenue are important and crucial to everything. Dix or D.C though is my favourite ( who doesn't love a kick arse princess) and really shines in this one. She's not perfect but she is unstoppable which I love.<br /><br />The plot is pretty standard really for YA fiction. There's not a lot of surprises or twists it turns and mostly you can see what's coming but that's fine.<br />The dialogue deserves a special mention as it will make you laugh, Snicker, cry and scream. It's brilliantly done and phenomenal writing. So witty, so biting, so cutting, so so good <br /><br />I will say though this one ramped up the violence and mayhem to the max. There's a bit in the others but it went way up here. It was over the top but in a good way. <br />It very much reminded me of professional wrestling which I'm s big fan of.<br />Scripted to a tried and tested formula it may be but it's always always entertaining.<br />You just can't turn away even though you know what's going to happen. Soapies use the same formula. People just get hooked by it.<br /><br />So an amazing series comes to an end but hopefully not final conclusion.<br />I really hope we see more from this series as it's too great not to see again.<br /><br />Cannot recommend it highly enough.<br />A must read for lovers of YA and fantasy fiction.</span>
  <a data-text-id="95285013869270143" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2424806842?book_show_action=true">Apr 10, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Justina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Justina" href="/user/show/67915326-justina">Justina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer2424806842&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2424806842" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15808776588179663456">Okay... Um...what the hell just happened.<br/><br/>After reading the 5 books apart of this series, I finally now know how it all ends. <br/><br/>Firstly, there wasn't a single dull moment in this novel, I almost read it all in one sitting because I couldn't stop, I was so eager to find out what would happen. <br/><br/><br/>After everything, Alex did save the world and the hardships she endured, and her friends and family literally dying before she went back in time to save them, we didn't really get to see a proper reunion betwee</span>
  <span id="freeText15808776588179663456" style="display:none">Okay... Um...what the hell just happened.<br /><br />After reading the 5 books apart of this series, I finally now know how it all ends. <br /><br />Firstly, there wasn't a single dull moment in this novel, I almost read it all in one sitting because I couldn't stop, I was so eager to find out what would happen. <br /><br /><br />After everything, Alex did save the world and the hardships she endured, and her friends and family literally dying before she went back in time to save them, we didn't really get to see a proper reunion between her friends, or how she was going to deal with all the trauma. It ended with her being applauded by everyone, and then it was done. So I do wish we had a little more, but then again it was a solid ending to an amazing series. <br /><br />The number of people who sacrificed their lives for this battle, the number of people who died and got tortured by this man, Aven. The preparation she had to defeat him for everything he did. So yes I was pretty disappointed to find out that Aven's punishment was being locked away in a painting in the Library? This guy was literally EATING people's hearts, he was torturing and manipulating people in the most horrific ways, but Alex gave her reasons and I guess being trapped in a painting isolated from everyone for the rest of your life is still adequate enough.<br /><br />(Also, I still think Aven was being a little dramatic because Aven got rejected by a mortal who he thought was immortal, and therefore felt embarrassed that he'd been lied to so he decided to literally kill the entire human race as well as everyone Alex loves... just me?)<br /><br />But these don't excuse how amazing it has been to read this series, and how much I love these characters, and what a journey it's been. So a solid 4 stars, because the pros outweigh the cons, and I enjoyed this so much and it makes me so sad to finish this series, but I can't wait until the author releases more books in this world, because I adore it. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15808776588179663456" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer7381972076385855256">Yes, FINALLY.<br/><br/>I have literally put this book off since it came out.<br/><br/>Unfortunately I was disappointed by Graevale. I read that book twice to see if I changed my mind but I didn't. That resulted me in almost dnf'ing this series, don't get me wrong - I've enjoyed this series along the way, but I just didn't have motivation to continue after feeling very bitter about the penultimate book.<br/><br/>I'm glad I decided to push myself to read this book in the end. Vardaesia is not the perfect finale, but I genuinel</span>
  <span id="freeText7381972076385855256" style="display:none">Yes, FINALLY.<br /><br />I have literally put this book off since it came out.<br /><br />Unfortunately I was disappointed by Graevale. I read that book twice to see if I changed my mind but I didn't. That resulted me in almost dnf'ing this series, don't get me wrong - I've enjoyed this series along the way, but I just didn't have motivation to continue after feeling very bitter about the penultimate book.<br /><br />I'm glad I decided to push myself to read this book in the end. Vardaesia is not the perfect finale, but I genuinely appreciate it. I loved Alex's character development in this book the most out of all books in the series. I felt the most connected to her here.<br /><br />This being said, I do find it a little unfortunate that character and plot development of this degree mostly happened in the 5th book of a 5-book series. A lot of this was slow burn, but I think things could have been pushed further by this point. I think this book could have been darker and pushed limits even more (but then again this series is meant to be family-friendly for the most part, so I do understand).<br /><br />In summary, a good conclusion but I'm relieved this isn't the end of possibilities in the Medoran world.</span>

<div id="review_2756656000" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2756656000" />
    <a title="Blue" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/70806132-blue"><img alt="Blue" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1567253168p2/70806132.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2756656000?book_show_action=true">Mar 25, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Blue" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Blue" href="/user/show/70806132-blue">Blue</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/40197450-vardaesia">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer2756656000&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2756656000" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4137654540973404460">So I decided to write the review as I read the book.. bit of a change but at the same time.. not much.<br/><br/>Let's start the book by talking abut how amazing Alex is.<br/>Ohh look more amazing Alex notes<br/>Ohh the battles was hard.... for everyone but Alex<br/>Better get help from a new far off place..<br/>Better talk about her scale skin again that is magically hidden all the time. Like her secret sword, her amazing combat skills. Like seriously how much can one character be truly blessed with all the gifts... she isn'</span>
  <span id="freeText4137654540973404460" style="display:none">So I decided to write the review as I read the book.. bit of a change but at the same time.. not much.<br /><br />Let's start the book by talking abut how amazing Alex is.<br />Ohh look more amazing Alex notes<br />Ohh the battles was hard.... for everyone but Alex<br />Better get help from a new far off place..<br />Better talk about her scale skin again that is magically hidden all the time. Like her secret sword, her amazing combat skills. Like seriously how much can one character be truly blessed with all the gifts... she isn't bloody Dumbledore<br />Again Alex has to prove herself worthy... what a shock. Let me guess we spend the whole book trying to prove how worthy she is?<br />Oh look she is put into a skimpy outfit like a fake wonder woman... gotta get that sex appeal. <br />**Side note though... I mean if some strangers came into your land and you want them to battle it out why are you going to dress them up like a sexy wonder woman? Stick them in the pit with the clothes they already have on... or maybe in some jelly and have them naked wrestle... just saying...<br />Alex having internal struggles.. ohhh noooo the silver platter life is soo hard and stressful.<br />But still dressed like royalty... Umm bitch you're an intruder... why is she always treated like a queen?<br />Playful banter is dulll like a dead bird.. none of the characters original sparks are in this book. Where is the original banter? I feel as though this has all been said before?<br />Over explaining... Again<br />Oh look Alex is having internal struggles again....<br />Ooops need to mention how amazing Alex is with her training and the tests Niyx put her through and her Meyarin blood.. Again<br />Seriously why did NIxy die... He was one character I loved.<br />3 pages on planning to climb the mountain.. 3 whole pages.<br />Of course the challenge has survival kits and water along the way. Wouldn't want the precious characters to actually struggle. Still climbing the mountain by the way..<br />Isn't there a war going on? I love how the war pauses for the characters to undergo challenges. War is sitting back and having a tea break while Alex is on a mission to prove herself.<br />Oh look they keep beating challenges how is Alex this amazing all the time. Doesn't her body burst for all this awesomeness<br />Over explaining..<br />Another friend betrayal but it's okay they still love each other... this will happen ten more times.<br />Ohh look the challenges of Alex and her friends proving herself is still ongoing like I thought it would.<br />Alex fighting a warrior with a blade and winning.. All young teenagers do right??<br />Page 244 still carrying out the test... War is just casually waiting for Alex to prove herself... Again<br />Oh look her friends get kidnapped... Who will save them? Oh no!<br />I like Aven he should be allowed to kill Alex, you know just as a side note.<br />Oh nooo they have her parents too... How is this possible<br />Ohhh Alex rescues everyone. Who would have thought<br />The dragon Xira dies but Alex lives... What fucked up shit is this.. she must be able to reverse time or something<br />Oh wait she legit just changed time... wow she might be a better wizard then Dumbledore after all.<br />Ohh look now everyone is saved.<br />Glad those last what 50 pages were saved for the battle...<br /><br />Don't get me wrong I fricken love Lynette's writing style and will be purchasing her other series as it comes out (I still have yet to read Whisper) but what bugs me is the character and story flaws in this book. All the gifts are given to Alex. All the challenges are easy for Alex. She doesn't seem to struggle and this is setting up the wrong kinda image, life aint this damn easy and it would have been nice for other characters to actually have some awesome stuff happen to them instead of the oh favourite Alex. I would literally have given this book a 5 stars if Aven stabbed Alex in the head with a fork...<br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_2895411397" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2895411397" />
    <a title="Ashlyn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/20809773-ashlyn"><img alt="Ashlyn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420430326p2/20809773.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2895411397?book_show_action=true">Jul 27, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ashlyn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ashlyn" href="/user/show/20809773-ashlyn">Ashlyn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20809773-ashlyn?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20809773-ashlyn?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2895411397" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer236682012342702879">4.5 stars (seriously goodreads when are you going to bring in the half stars?)<br/><br/>If you haven’t read this series yet, go now. Go buy this series and start reading!<br/><br/>I still can’t believe how much I love this series! Book 1 just didn’t do this adventure justice. It’s been a while since I almost hesitantly read the last page of a book, not wanting to bring these characters and story to a close. I adored everything about this last book. It had everything a conclusion needed to satisfy. High stakes? Chec</span>
  <span id="freeText236682012342702879" style="display:none">4.5 stars (seriously goodreads when are you going to bring in the half stars?)<br /><br />If you haven’t read this series yet, go now. Go buy this series and start reading!<br /><br />I still can’t believe how much I love this series! Book 1 just didn’t do this adventure justice. It’s been a while since I almost hesitantly read the last page of a book, not wanting to bring these characters and story to a close. I adored everything about this last book. It had everything a conclusion needed to satisfy. High stakes? Check. Tears of joy and heartache? Check. Adventure? Check. A fierce final battle? Double check.<br /><br />These characters have grown so much and the new ones introduced along the way only served to better the story. In the end there were so many characters I loved it was impossible for them all to get enough page time. After their noticeable absence in book 4 I was beyond excited to see both Xira and Roka again.<br />Alex is one of the best heroines I’ve read about in a while. At no stage did she become irritating or mind numbingly stupid in her decision making (I find this a common trait amongst YA fantasy heroines). Even when she and Kaiden finally got together she was focused on her responsibilities and I love that she didn’t just become love struck and incapable of still being herself. She was so strong but also vulnerable and it made her so endearing. I loved her character growth and was really impressed with her overall storyline.<br />I still feel a little indifferent to her human friends (except Bear I have a soft spot for him). D.C was just meh and Jordan got really annoying. Her immortal friends however were the true sidekicks of the story. The Meyarins, the Draekorans, the Tia Aurans, I found them all so fascinating. However Niyx will forever remain the best character in the Medoran Chronicles.<br />Is it terrible that I still feel some semblance of affection for Aven? He’s a terrible monster beyond forgiveness but I still ache at the memory of who he once was and it makes me so sad. But he was irredeemable and I’m glad Lynette Noni didn’t attempt to redeem him. He was too far gone but I miss the Aven he once was.<br /><br />I also loved that even though we were in the final book there was still time for one more adventure. I found Tia Auras wildly interesting and a refreshing detour that still contributed to the story. The gates of testing were awesome, moving us forward whilst also reminding us of all the past plot points that have shaped these books. It was also exciting knowing they would eventually return to Medora and face Aven one final time.<br /><br />Lynette Noni you finished this series with the promise of returning to Medora. I don’t need to know any details I will just be there. </span>
  <a data-text-id="236682012342702879" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2705645389" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2705645389" />
    <a title="Emily" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8753325-emily"><img alt="Emily" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1501074922p2/8753325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2705645389?book_show_action=true">Feb 21, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily" href="/user/show/8753325-emily">Emily</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8753325-emily?shelf=the-ya-circle">the-ya-circle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8753325-emily?shelf=2019">2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8753325-emily?shelf=authors-i-have-met">authors-i-have-met</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2705645389" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17778037742484133176">All up I really enjoyed the final book in The Medoran Chronicles along with the rest of the series, however there were a few things in 'Vardaesia' that I didn't like as much. A main thing that didn't sit well with me was the pacing of the book <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Most of the book is set in Vardaesia (they are there until page 324, which I understand as that is the title of the book and I enjoyed reading about their time in Vardaesia. However, once Alex and co get back to fight Aven everything happen</span></span>
  <span id="freeText17778037742484133176" style="display:none">All up I really enjoyed the final book in The Medoran Chronicles along with the rest of the series, however there were a few things in 'Vardaesia' that I didn't like as much. A main thing that didn't sit well with me was the pacing of the book <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Most of the book is set in Vardaesia (they are there until page 324, which I understand as that is the title of the book and I enjoyed reading about their time in Vardaesia. However, once Alex and co get back to fight Aven everything happens so quickly. I think a part of what made it feel rushed were the lists of names of the dead. Lyn just seemed to wrap up everything rather neatly and quickly, especially in the contexts of how much of the book was spent in another world. It just didn't really seem balanced to me. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Another thing that I didn't like was how on numerous occasions there seemed to be a few lines missing <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ When Alex talks to other characters and makes plans the conversation would stop abruptly, generally missing out of the key step of the plan. I get that it means the plans are a secret until the event occurs (possibly intended to create drama and suspense), nevertheless, it felt as if segments were missing.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. On a more positive note, I love some of the new characters we are introduced to in this book. And I still ship Declan and Bear!! It was a bittersweet read at times as well, in particular at any mention of Niyx (and Xira (and Kaiden too I guess)) - why all my favourite characters from this series are guys I do not really know. <br /><br />The reason why my rating is so high is because I love Lyn as a person (and as an author) and I have really enjoyed reading this series. If Lyn wasn't the author I think my rating may be lower.</span>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13970559740865323526">**EDIT** now review embargo has been lifted I can share more of my thoughts..<br/><br/>It was an amazing finish to a great series and I found the ending to be quite clever, not what I had expected but I also feel it’s left it open.. I believe there is scope for more but hey that’s just me.. I loved how the book tied in the series together but embarked on a whole new adventure of 6 tests/gates - each leaving me on the edge of my seat and the interesting twists of getting introduced to new and exciting char</span>
  <span id="freeText13970559740865323526" style="display:none">**EDIT** now review embargo has been lifted I can share more of my thoughts..<br /><br />It was an amazing finish to a great series and I found the ending to be quite clever, not what I had expected but I also feel it’s left it open.. I believe there is scope for more but hey that’s just me.. I loved how the book tied in the series together but embarked on a whole new adventure of 6 tests/gates - each leaving me on the edge of my seat and the interesting twists of getting introduced to new and exciting characters whilst continuing the adventure with long standing characters. I even had a tear in my eye with one part of the book too. It is a bitter sweet feeling to see this great series come to an end but never say never. Fast paced read, definitely held my attention to the end, a beautiful finish.. many thanks again to Pantera Press Publishers for giving me an advanced review copy at Kaldoras Dinner last year!!<br /><br />- - - <br /><br />Reviews embargoed until release date. Special thanks to Pantera Press Publishers for giving me an advanced review copy at Kaldoras Dinner!! [full review will be posted here and on blog - stay tuned]<br /><br /></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2635669062" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2635669062?book_show_action=true">Dec 23, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

  <span id="freeText5803770304613803953" style="display:none">This book finished the Medoran Chronicles on a really high note. It had twists and turns that I totally did not see coming, my heart stopped many times when reading this book and seriously, it has all the feels that a human can handle. Be prepared for all the heart and wonder that you expect to experience from the previous novels. I loved that it ties up all the books in this series really well. For Alex, the stakes are higher than ever and I have absolutely enjoyed spending time with our favourite characters from the novel. I’m having withdraw symptoms because it’s the final book. My recommendation is to relish every moment in this book. It is everything that I needed in a final book and so much more! The Medoran chronicles overall is a story of hope, friendship and love, with great themes, plot twists and characters that you’ll wish are real. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14601586266902399036">I am in love with this serie! I wish I had a sentient Library :)<br/><br/>I went through it all during these 5,5 books (but really 6), I laughed and I cried like I haven't in a while, and I am so happy for it!<br/><br/>I had be looking out to the end of this serie for years, and now I'm so happy (as you can see I'm really happy) to learn that there will be more.   <span id="freeText14601586266902399036" style="display:none">I am in love with this serie! I wish I had a sentient Library :)<br /><br />I went through it all during these 5,5 books (but really 6), I laughed and I cried like I haven't in a while, and I am so happy for it!<br /><br />I had be looking out to the end of this serie for years, and now I'm so happy (as you can see I'm really happy) to learn that there will be more. The story is not over, Alex's story has ended, but there will be new adventures!<br /><br />While I was reading We Three Heroes, I found myself crying because the stories of D.C., Jordan, and Bear were so heartbreaking, but then I realized that I was feeling so bad because these characters had become my friends and I couldn't be there for them. This is something that never happened to me, at least not like that. I laughed at their jokes, imagined that they would laugh at mine, and they became my friends.<br /><br />In her acknowledgments, Lynette Noni thanked every person that spread the word about her books and those that "sometimes throw them into hands and/or faces", and that's what I want to to do, I wish I could put them into people's hand and shove them in their faces :) But I can't, so here's why you should read them:<br />- The characters feel so real, so normal (despite their gifts), and I love them so much. Alex has more endurance, physical and emotional, than you can imagine, I would curled into a ball crying at the end of Akarnae :)<br />- There is a sentient Library that offers more than books<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Literature may increase one’s depth of knowledge, but not all knowledge be found in literature. Only with practical experience can one truly learn and thus be considered knowledgeable.”</i>
</blockquote><br />- Lynette Noni is friends with Sarah J. Maas (I feel like it's a selling argument, ha ha!)<br /><br />I feel like I always come short when I try to explain why a book is so great, so go read it, pleeeeaaaase! You will love it!<br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9940374656668579880"><br/>This book was an amazing conclusion to an AMAZING series. I loved how the book was unpredictable and not your typical, we need help, we’ll help you, oh look we won! It was just so immersive and captivating and I just couldn’t wait to turn the page. Even though the events of this series are centred around magic and otherworldly adventures Lynette Noni still manages to make the characters reactions to everything so relatable and that’s why I love this series and this book so much!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/HOKHRmxALOY54iPTPOGiF9ILG5KuCnBlLUBEdIBjDs4z0GcDqiby1pBVZ51x0cUIO8eZHVd4nfxXIF/RGm74A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EQs/XkDp3LZ+QLqFKzby90Mt1tSt7o7wKVFHHniBLQjVt/TfV/BHzrzmZ5QSAjNrPIrk3pILRUZMuMdw7uka0w==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer10801207971775270834">Lynette Noni studied journalism and academic writing at university before completing a degree in human behavior. She lives on the Sunshine Coast in Australia and can be found baking cupcakes, singing along to animated movies, or daydreaming about being swept away to a fantasy world. Some days, she can even do all three at once — and still find the time to sneak in a nap afterwards. </span>

        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('bookCover_35439559').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('bookCover_35439559').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_35439559').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
</div>
